Unexpectedly, Lin Zhisong has recently changed his behavior, not returning home at night. Lin Qiu felt that her husband was behaving strangely, so she investigated and learned that he had another woman. Lin Qiu saw her husband going astray and was deeply concerned, so she gently advised him to change. However, Lin Zhisong not only did not realize his error, but instead harbored resentment and treated his wife like a thorn in his side, frequently verbally and physically abusing her, showing no marital affection. Now, Lin Zhisong has hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit in the First Special District Local Court, requesting permission to divorce Qiu Axiu. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Peng Shi presided over the hearing in the Civil Court No. 14. Both the plaintiff and defendant arrived in court with their lawyers. According to the plaintiff Lin Zhisong's statement, the defendant Lin Qiu does not uphold the virtues of a wife and often goes out gambling and wandering. On the fifth day of the first lunar month, she ran away from home. At first, he did not suspect anything, but after waiting for three days and not seeing her return, he reported it to the police, which is on record. Therefore, he requests a divorce. Subsequently, according to the defendant Qiu Axiu, on the fifth day of the first lunar month, she went to visit her maternal uncle's house for the New Year and stayed overnight. When she returned home the next morning, she found that the door was locked. Upon asking the plaintiff's mother, she was told that Lin Zhisong had taken the key and said that she had been sued in court and did not need to return home. Seeing this situation, she had no choice but to return to her mother's house to stay temporarily. She does not want to divorce the plaintiff and requests that the divorce lawsuit be rejected. The lawyers for both sides then debated each other to the end. Judge Peng then adjourned the court and announced that the verdict would be pronounced on the afternoon of the 10th.

After Killing Robbers, Stray Bullet Kills a British Man: Fierce Battle Between Detectives and Robbers Behind Hongkou Police Station; Municipal Council Laborer Zhu Amao Seriously Injured 152

Yesterday morning at around 6:00 AM, three young men arrived at the Zhongshan Automobile Company at the intersection of Gongping Road and Broadway Road in Hongkou, claiming that they wanted to rent a car to go to Yuanchang Road. The company assigned Jiangbei native Wen Dingxin as the driver to drive car No. 12608, which was registered in the foreign settlement. On the way, the young men instructed the driver to stop at the entrance of Yuanchang Lane on Yuanchang Road. Upon reaching the destination, the three men got out of the car one after another and walked into the lane, telling the driver to wait outside. The driver assumed they were visiting friends, so he did not pay attention. Unexpectedly, the young men were actually robbers. After walking into the lane, they went straight to the home of Wang Shiting (a native of Taixing), a traditional Chinese medicine surgeon at No. 16. They drew their pistols, knocked on the door, and went inside. They went upstairs and broke into Wang's bedroom. Wang had not yet gotten out of bed, so he was unable to resist and allowed them to search the room. However, Wang's eldest son, Wang Quan, who was 15 years old, had already gotten up. Seeing that the visitors were up to no good, he quickly ran to the balcony, crossed the rooftops, and escaped to a neighbor's house to report the incident and ask for help. As a result, the neighbors went with him to report to the gatekeeper, and the gatekeeper blew the whistle to alert the police. Police officers in the vicinity heard the alarm and rushed to the scene. As they were preparing to enter the lane to surround and arrest the robbers, the robbers noticed them. They grabbed the stolen goods and fled from the house. Two of the robbers fled east, while one robber ran to the entrance of the lane, jumped into the car, and forced the driver to drive at full speed and flee west. The police officers saw the robbers fleeing in the car, so they chased after them, drawing their guns and shooting at the car. The robber in the car fired back at the police officers. Gunshots rang out, and bullets flew like beads. When they reached the Pengpu Road intersection, the car's rear tire was shot out by the police officers, making it difficult to drive. The robbers ordered the driver to stop the car immediately. However, the car was traveling at high speed, and when the driver suddenly slammed on the brakes, the car swerved and crashed into the sidewalk. At that moment, the robber jumped out of the car and fled towards the Hongkou triangle market on Miller Road. However, seeing that the police officers were about to catch up, he turned around and fired again while running, retreating into the area behind the Hongkou police station. The police officers also arrived and engaged in a fierce battle. The robber was shot four times in the body and once in the head, and he collapsed to the ground due to his injuries and died on the spot. However, during the fierce battle, it so happened that McDonald, the British foreman of the lathe department of the Ruirong Iron Factory, was passing by on Miller Road. Unable to avoid the stray bullets, he was struck in the brain and abdomen. He died at the same time behind the Hongkou police station. He was a truly tragic victim. Also, a Municipal Council Public Works Department laborer named Zhu Amao was injured by a stray bullet. His injuries were very serious, and his life may be in danger. He was sent to the Municipal Council hospital for treatment by the police car. The robber's body was sent to the coroner's office for an autopsy. The body of the British man McDonald was reported to the British Consulate for an autopsy and arrangements for his funeral. Regarding the loss of the victim, it was estimated to be over one hundred gold pieces. The police believed that the car driver's actions were suspicious, so he was temporarily detained for investigation.

Tan Boying Discusses Recent Developments in the Ferry Business: Construction of Ferry No. 6; Taking Over the Seaside Bathing Resort 153

The Shanghai Industrial Trust Company Ferry Management Office has been experiencing significant growth in its business recently. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Mr. Tan Boying, the manager of the company, yesterday to inquire about the situation. Mr. Tan described the recent business conditions as follows:

Ferry No. 6

The municipal ferry has been operating night cruises in the summer for many years, and tourists are very crowded. The original ferries were not enough to accommodate them. In addition, the company has also been requested by major shipping companies to pick up and drop off passengers from ocean liners. Long-term contracts have been signed with the Zha Hua Company, and other companies have also come to hire ferries due to the company's thoughtful service. The company has been hesitant to agree because there were not enough ferries, recognizing the urgent need for these two items, they will build a special Ferry No. 6. All designs are similar to Ferry No. 5, and the magnificent is even more so. It has been under construction for several months and will be completed in the summer.

Seaside Bathing Resort

The Gaoqiao Seaside Bathing Resort, located outside the seawall of the East Beach, has a natural sandy beach that is the only place for Chinese and Westerners in Shanghai to rest in the summer. Its business has always been owned by the Gaoqiao Seaside Hotel. This year, the hotel is focusing on the hotel business and is willing to transfer the bathing resort business to the company. The company is requesting approval from the municipal government and is focusing on sorting it out. Inside the seawall, there will be mud dredging to create a dam and water will be introduced to make tides. It will be divided into two parts, inside and outside, with a small bridge in the middle for boating. Trees will be planted on the shore, and the situation will be like a small West Lake. In addition, houses will be built for men's and women's changing rooms, showers, restaurants, kitchens, etc. The green tiles and red walls are full of wild fun and are also expected to be completed in the summer. The company has also requested the Municipal Public Works Bureau to widen the road to the seaside, as it is too narrow, to avoid traffic accidents. The cost will be borne by the company.

Floating Hotel

Since its opening, the Floating Hotel at the company's Beijing Road pier has been crowded with women, breaking the record for newly opened hotels. Every day, no less than one hundred people are turned away due to lack of seating. The company has had to expand the special waiting room into a dining room and convert the original office into a waiting room. The office will have to be moved to the lower level.

The Major Fishery Market, built by the Ministry of Industry in Yangshupu, Shanghai, has been under construction since last year. After several consultations between Hua Yinchun of the Fishery Market Preparatory Office and the company, the contract was formally signed yesterday morning. The construction of the cold storage will be divided into four parts: (1) cold storage, (2) ice making, (3) freezing, and (4) machinery. The ice-making part will be completed in advance by mid-July in order to adapt to the seasonal needs. It can produce 410 "担" of ice per day for sale. Eight companies, including the Jiangnan Shipyard, have submitted bids for the floating pier project. The deadline is today, and the bids will be submitted to the ministry for approval and award. Construction will begin soon. The entire project of the Fishery Market will be completed between September and October of this year.

Truck Driver's Negligence Leads to Death of Garbage Cart Driver 159

The case was inspected by the court and prosecuted by the police. Bai Xuehuai, a native of Jiancheng County, Jiangbei, 21 years old, lived at No. 129 Malan Road in the French Concession. He worked as a garbage cart pusher for the Shanghai Municipal Council in the Public Concession. In the early morning of the previous day, at around 5:00 AM, Bai was pushing cart No. 8 on the east side of Yuyuan Road, heading east on the north side of the road. Another garbage cart, No. 10, pushed by Guo Shimin, was also traveling west on the south side of the road. Unexpectedly, a truck with license plate No. 9778 from the Tanle Motor Company, driven by Gu Sihai, sped up from behind Guo's cart. Seeing the impending collision, Gu attempted to avoid it by turning the truck north. However, due to his lack of driving skills, he instead crashed into garbage cart No. 8 and severely injured Bai. The Jing'an Temple police station received a report and immediately dispatched detectives to apprehend Gu and bring him to the police station. They also summoned an ambulance to rush the injured Bai to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he died shortly after. The body was transported to the autopsy center on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, the police first escorted Gu to the First Special District Court and filed a public prosecution according to the law, requesting an extension of the case pending autopsy results. At around 10:00 AM, Prosecutor Tang, appointed by the Prosecutor's Office, along with Forensic Doctor Wei, Clerk Wang Zuyi, and others, arrived at the autopsy center to examine the body. After confirming the body, they took their seats for the official case. The Western police first reported the previous events, stating that the road was approximately 32.2 feet wide. At the time, garbage cart No. 10 was about 5.6 feet from the street edge, and cart No. 8 was about 4.6 feet from the street edge. Therefore, the truck's passage on the road should not have resulted in a collision, indicating the driver's negligence in causing the accident. They therefore filed a lawsuit in accordance with the law. Prosecutor Tang then briefly interrogated the witness Guo Shimin and the truck driver Gu Sihai. It was then decreed that the deceased, Bai Xuehuai, a male, had indeed died from injuries sustained from being struck by truck No. 9778. In addition to the truck driver Gu Sihai being suspected of professional negligence resulting in death, since the family of the deceased had not yet arrived, the body was temporarily handed over to the Pushan Villa for preservation.

Fei, together with Zhang Xiaomao, a Haimen native watching the alley at No. 25 Zhengyuan Lane, Beidi Road, dragged Lin into the middle of the road and beat her, causing injuries to the back of her head and abdomen. The attackers fled the scene. Later, Sister Han Si and others helped Lin up and sent her to her employer's house, falsely claiming that she had been hit by a car. Recognizing her grave responsibility

Abandoned the corpse

Assisting in injury

Causing death, to seven years of imprisonment and deprivation of public rights for seven years. Fang Lin and Luo Geng were acquitted. Ni Jikuan, the husband of the deceased Ni Lin, received news from his hometown in Hefei and rushed to Shanghai. Based on what he was told by fellow villagers Xu Shaoqing (unemployed, residing at No. 137 Pushi Road), Wang Peiyin (tailor, residing at No. 6 Albert Road), and his wife's fellow villagers, Sister Han Si and Sister Wang (both residing at No. 137 Pushi Road, where the deceased went to hang out the night of the incident, which led to the disaster), that Little Cifantuan Fei Jinhai, Zhang Xiaomao, and others, were

Residing on Pushi Road

And were instigated to assault and cause death by Xiao A Mei, Bao San, Liang Du, A Xing, and the owner of Shunxing Water and Electricity Company at No. 128 Pushi Road, and the owner of Yuanmaosheng Hotel at No. 135 Pushi Road. Furthermore, the employer Chen Li did not agree to send her to the hospital or pay her wages at the time, deliberately abandoning her, resulting in her death, etc. Ni Jikuan immediately reported this to the French police station, requesting their arrest and interrogation. The police station rejected the report because Ni's report was based entirely on empty claims and lacked any supporting evidence. Ni, still not satisfied, hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Criminal Court of the Second Special Court, accusing Xiao A Mei, Bao San, Liang Du, A Xing, the owner of Shunxing Water and Electricity Company, the owner of Yuanmaosheng Hotel, and the employer Chen Li, etc., seven people, of

Inciting injury

Abandonment, etc., requesting their trial, and attached a civil suit, seeking compensation for the coffin transportation back to his hometown for burial of five hundred yuan, and compensation for lost wages of nine hundred and fifty yuan, totaling one thousand four hundred and fifty yuan, to be borne jointly by the defendants, Little Cifantuan, and Zhang Xiaomao. The court accepted the complaint, and yesterday, Judge Zhang Chaozuo opened the Second Criminal Court to summon the parties. The plaintiff Ni Jikuan, accompanied by a lawyer, and witnesses Xu Shaoqing, Wang Peiyin, Han Si, and Wang, four men and women, arrived at the court. The first three defendants, Xiao A Mei, Bao San, and Liang Du, did not arrive. A Xing (surnamed Zhang, only eleven years old), Wang Youwen, the owner of Shunxing Water and Electricity Company, Chen Guanghan, the owner of Yuanmaosheng Hotel, and Chen Li, four people, were summoned to the court. Ni Jikuan, the plaintiff, first stated his

Reasons for the lawsuit

The judge said to Ni, "The murderers Fei Jinhai and Zhang Xiaomao have already been convicted. Now you are accusing seven defendants, even including the child and the employer. Who exactly instigated the crime? Causing death is a serious matter and cannot be accused lightly." Ni claimed, "The witnesses told me. I was in the countryside at the time. After receiving the news, I came to Shanghai to investigate the matter. Xu Shaoqing, Wang Peiyin, and the other four witnesses told me. Otherwise, I am unfamiliar with this place and do not know the defendants, so how would I know the details?" The judge then questioned the defendant Zhang A and obtained his testimony. "I was not at the scene when they fought at No. 135 Pushi Road." Wang Youwen, the owner of Shunxing Water and Electricity Company (with a pockmarked face), testified, "I was not in the shop when the fight occurred. When I returned to the shop, the fight had already ended. I saw a patrolman and

Two foreigners

Came, and a car was parked nearby. Later, I saw the person who had been beaten get into the car and leave towards Avenue Joffre." Chen Guanghan, the owner of Yuanmaosheng Hotel, operated his hotel downstairs at No. 135 Pushi Road. The upstairs was occupied by people from Anhui, whom he did not know. He had something to attend to when the fight broke out and only returned at around 1:00 AM, when he learned about the fight. These three all denied instigating the beating. Chen Li testified, "Ni Lin worked as a servant in my house for only twenty-one days. That evening, after dinner, she went out without even washing the dishes. At around 9:00 PM, three women brought her back, saying that she had been hit in the back of the head by a car and had toothpaste applied to it. I said I would send her to the hospital, but they refused to go. Since she was living in my house, it was inconvenient, so I asked the person living with me to notify the employment agency, and the

The landlady

Came to take her away." After the testimony was completed, a written statement was presented to the court. At this point, the judge summoned the witness Xu Shaoqing, who testified, "I am blind in one eye and cannot see clearly. At the time, I only saw many people fighting. Wang Peiyin told me that a pockmarked face told them to hit him. So I knew that the pockmarked face was the owner of Shunxing Water and Electricity Company." Wang Peiyin testified, "At the time, I was upstairs and saw Little Cifantuan fighting with a pockmarked face. Another pockmarked face, i.e., the owner of Shunxing Water and Electricity Company, was standing nearby yelling at them to fight. He did not lay a hand on them himself. I did not see the child A Xing there." Sister Wang testified, "I lived on the upper floor of Yuanmaosheng Hotel. That night, Ni Lin came, stood on the handrail, holding a teacup. Someone below said that water had splashed on them and cursed. Little Cifantuan then came up and took Ni Lin's

Teacup from her hand

Ni Lin also cursed back and went downstairs, and was then grabbed and beaten by them. I rushed out to persuade them, and it was Little Cifantuan and Little Mao who were beating her. Seeing the patrolman coming, they fled. Wang Youwen was standing nearby yelling at them to fight. The hotel owner and A Xing were standing on the side. Later, I accompanied Ni Lin to her employer's house. Chen Li refused to send her to the hospital and also refused to pay her wages." Sister Wang's testimony was the same as Sister Han Si's. The judge then asked the plaintiff Ni Jikuan if he had anything else to say. Ni claimed, "Now that the person is dead and the coffin cannot be transported back for burial, I myself cannot even go home. I ask the court to be the judge." The judge said, "Two individuals have already been convicted in this case. You

Want to extort money

You won't be able to get it. Shanghai is different from the county magistrate's office in the interior. In the countryside, you can threaten people for money, and if you don't get the money, you sue them. You can seek damages from the two already convicted, but you can't just randomly accuse seven defendants based on empty words." The lawyer representing the plaintiff then supplemented his opinion. The court ruled that the defendants were not all present and the case required further investigation. The fifth defendant, Wang Youwen, the owner of Shunxing Water and Electricity Company, was ordered to provide a guarantor who could be summoned at any time, or else he would be detained. The lawyer representing the plaintiff was also informed that the names of the fifth and sixth defendants, the owner of Shunxing Water and Electricity Company and the owner of Yuanmaosheng Hotel, were not listed on the complaint, which did not comply with legal procedure, and that a supplementary complaint should be submitted to the court for further summons. The court adjourned after this.

Since the China Anti-Tuberculosis Association launched a campaign to discourage spitting in this city, and organized publicity campaigns among various sectors of the academic, business, and community groups, it has been able to arouse the attention of the general public in this city. Lu Bohong's Model Asylum Completely Completed; Construction Costs 500,000 Yuan; Accepting Patients from the 1st of Next Month 164

Lu Bohong, a great philanthropist in this city, recognized the lack of large-scale mental hospitals in the country, causing those suffering from mental illnesses to have nowhere to seek medical treatment. Therefore, he invested in the establishment of a model asylum, which has now been completed and is scheduled to start accepting patients on the first of next month. The details are as follows:

Complete Completion: The hospital is located in Beiqiao Town, this city, covering an area of more than ten acres. Construction began in the autumn of last year, and the project was fully completed at the end of March this year. It is named Puji Sanatorium. The hospital is located in a secluded area with fresh air and no noise from vehicles, making it a perfect place for patients to recuperate. The construction cost a total of 500,000 yuan, not including equipment costs.

Accepting Patients: The hospital is large in scale and can accommodate 500 to 600 patients. The internal facilities are all arranged with reference to foreign sanatoriums, and the equipment purchased is also the latest. The doctors are half foreign and half Chinese, and they have been hired and are preparing to start accepting patients from the 1st of next month.

Dredging the Wusong River to Change to Using Dredgers for Construction; Shipping Will Resume as Soon as the Machines Arrive and the Dam is Opened 170

In order to dredge the Wusong River, the Taihu Lake Conservancy Commission broke the dam for work on April 1st in the area of Yujidun Zhuangjia Lane. However, half of the rice boats and manure boats in Shanghai came from this route. After the dam was broken, the rice boats had to take a detour around the Southern Huangpu River, which took three days longer than usual. The manure boats, because the boats were too small, could not detour around the big port. Therefore, in addition to farmers from the Zhenru Beixinjing area of Zhabei coming to Shanghai to buy, the other areas of Huangdu, Qingpu, etc., have completely disappeared, causing a yellow panic in Zhabei. The drivers, having nowhere to dump, dumped the manure into the Huangpu River and sewers. The Shanghai Municipal Government, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and the Nanjing Municipal Government believe that this matter is related to hygiene and endangers public order, so they negotiated with the Taihu Lake Conservancy Commission to change to using dredgers to dredge the river in order to maintain shipping. After the Taihu Lake Conservancy Commission submitted a request to the National Economic Commission for instructions, it was decided to use machine dredging. Once the authorities transport the machinery to Shanghai, the dam can be opened. The commission also announced to all sectors of society: "It is hereby announced that the project to dredge the Yujidun section of the Wusong River was previously scheduled to break the dam on April 1st and was announced in the newspapers. Now, in order to maintain ship traffic, it has been approved by the National Economic Commission to change to machine dredging. All sectors of society are hereby notified accordingly."

Last month, on the 6th, according to Inspector Li Qingjie of the Tanzi Bay Police Station under the Zhabei New Zha Sub-bureau, nine people, including gambling offender Yan Fusheng (also known as Yan Fusheng), were arrested and brought in. After Officer Ouyang Liu sentenced them to detention, Yan Fusheng died due to illness, which was reported in the newspapers. Now, it is learned that during the coroner's examination, the deceased's brother, Yan Lousheng, suspected that his brother's sudden death was suspicious. Therefore, Prosecutor Zhao Chuanjia immediately ordered the local guarantor, Li Ruiru, to transport the body to the Zhenru Forensic Autopsy Institute for an autopsy. Yesterday morning, Yan Lousheng suddenly filed a petition with the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office, accompanied by the deceased's wife, Qiao, stating that they had come to Shanghai from a remote area in Jiangbei and were in a hurry and panic, unaware of the truth. Therefore, they mistakenly claimed that the cause of death was unclear and raised doubts. They now know that the deceased, Yan Fusheng, died of suffocation due to phlegm and earnestly request exemption from sending the body to the Zhenru Autopsy Institute for an autopsy. After receiving the petition, Prosecutor Zhao, based on the repeated requests from the deceased's family for exemption from sending the body to the Zhenru Forensic Autopsy Institute for an autopsy, granted their request and issued a certificate stating that the deceased, Yan Fusheng, indeed died of illness and that the deceased's family could prepare a coffin for burial. Therefore, yesterday afternoon at 2:20 PM, the wife of the deceased took the body away for burial. The coffin has already been loaded onto a boat and transported back to Jiangbei for burial. The deceased is survived by a son and a daughter. The young son, named Gen Shun, is ten years old, and the elder daughter, named A Mao, is sixteen years old. It is also learned that among the nine gambling offenders in the same group, besides the deceased Yan Fusheng, there is also Wang Changfu, who is a member of the Fire Brigade. At that time, Director Ruan approved him to pay a fine in lieu of detention. The remaining seven people, Wang A Jin, Yuan A Bao, Liu A Er, Wang Xiao Sanzi, Xiao Dengjie, Yang Yingen, and Yang Fujun, were still detained at the Zhabei Branch of the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau yesterday afternoon.

American United Life Insurance Company Shareholders' Meeting 173

The American United Life Insurance Company held its annual shareholders' meeting at its headquarters on the Bund at number 17 yesterday. Mr. Starr, the chairman, read and approved the minutes of the previous meeting. The board of directors reported on the company's business performance last year. Fei Mengde, Bei Shiyi, Hu Leiwen, Xue Deshi, and Starr ((CV) Shi Kelei Starr (NV)) were re-elected as directors. The main points of the report were as follows: The company's business made considerable progress last year, with new business reaching 12,540,537.00 national currency. After deducting overdue policy surrenders and maturity refunds, the net profit was 3,559,189.56 yuan. The total effective insurance amount, as of November 31st last year, exceeded 56,683,892.79 Shanghai taels. Western life insurance actuaries have long debated the mortality rate of the Eastern population without reaching a consensus. According to statistics compiled over many years and recent data on the Japanese mortality rate, the general conclusion is that the mortality rate of the Far Eastern population is far higher than that of Europe and America. However, based on the experience of American United Life Insurance Company in China for the past fourteen years, this statement is not accurate. According to the company's analysis of the mortality rate of its policyholders, the conclusions are as follows: (1) In the recent two or three decades, due to the improvement of the lifestyle of Chinese people, the invention of modern medicine, the increase of hygiene knowledge, and the equipment of modern hospitals, the population mortality rate has indeed decreased, especially in the major cities where the company is located. Chinese people with good economic conditions and good health habits tend to live long lives and have a natural resistance to certain diseases that Westerners cannot match. (2) According to the company's fourteen years of experience, the average number of deaths is only 61% of the expected number, and only 60% last year. The reason why the performance is better than other companies is due to the perfection of doctors' examination equipment. Recently, Western companies have increased premiums or reduced dividends, but as a result of the lower mortality rate in the Far East, the collection of premiums may be reduced in the future. Insurance companies sprang up in the United States from 1845 to 1860 and have now become the largest and most powerful companies in the country. Last year, insurance companies also emerged in China and the Philippine Islands. Their future achievements are bound to be considerable. The company believes that this phenomenon is a manifestation of Eastern people gradually understanding the benefits of life insurance. The directors are convinced that constructive cooperation, rather than malicious protection or destructive competition, can promote the life insurance business in China. Therefore, within the scope of cooperation and assistance with the company, they will be encouraged and assisted to promote the entire life insurance business and benefit the countries where the business is located. Today is the 14th annual shareholders' meeting of American United Life Insurance Company. American United Life Insurance Company will have a history of fifteen years, so it can no longer be called a small life insurance company. Each year, the company not only gradually increases its business volume and stability, but also its organizational efficiency is increasing day by day. When the company started its business, life insurance was completely unknown in China. Therefore, at that time, the company's creation of this business in China was of great importance. Today, the company has become a financial institution, and the responsibilities borne by its directors are increasing day by day, and its service opportunities have gradually expanded. After carefully examining the accounts of this session, everyone knows that the profit for 1934 was 370,635.04 yuan. Compared with the profit of 403,964.32 yuan in 1933, we should be very satisfied, because 1934 was in a very economic situation. The company's cash position is also very stable. The amount of cash in stock and deposited in banks reached 677,043.04 yuan. The amount of assets increased by 1,369.23 yuan in one year, of which 232,358.99 yuan was borrowed by policyholders with policy pledges, and the rest was investment. The average interest rate of the main investment was 5.8%. The exchange difference was 48,201.78 yuan, which has been included in the profit account. This difference could have been included in the silver reserve account, but the auditors and directors advocated that, at this time of current currency instability, the original reserve should still be maintained. This difference occurred because of the temporary difference in currency values between Shanghai and Hong Kong after the implementation of the Chinese silver export micro-tax regulations. However, the gap between the currency systems will gradually balance through natural economic capacity and continued remittances from Hong Kong. Last year, excluding expenses, 204,151.91 yuan was accumulated. Adding this year's operating profit, and subtracting dividends, exchange differences, and taxes, the amount available for distribution and other expenses this year is 371,580.25 yuan. The directors believe that the company's profits should be distributed to shareholders, but under today's unstable situation, it is necessary to temporarily pay extra dividends until a more significant solution to Shanghai's economic problems is achieved. However, the dividends to which policyholders are entitled will continue to be distributed at the current amount. The loyalty and enthusiasm of the managers and staff are the company's most valuable assets. Finally, I have to say a few words to commend them.

Mogan Mountain is located in the northwest of Wukang County, Zhejiang Province, and is only two hours away from Hangzhou. The scenery is excellent. It is not only suitable for escaping the summer heat, but also for touring in late spring and early autumn. In April, the mountain flowers are just beginning to bloom, the climate is mild, and climbing the mountain is full of fun. Therefore, tourists to Hangzhou often take a detour to visit the mountain. However, finding scenic spots and exploring hidden places depends on a special guidebook, so that one can stroll leisurely with a walking stick and have a reliable guide. Special Announcement

Annual Business Report of Jin Cheng Bank for the Year 23 (27) 182

(C) Assisting Transportation Enterprises. The development of transportation enterprises is of profound importance to a country's economy. The Bank has always provided considerable services to railway transportation and also wants to help its engineering development and equipment improvement, so as to facilitate the circulation of products in the interior and make up for trade deficits externally, and promote the output of industries internally, so as to benefit the current economic situation of our country. The Bank's services to national roads this year, the major ones are as follows: (1) Loans for Construction. The Yuehan Railway is the main line connecting the north and south, the Tongxi Railway is the place where the products of the northwest gather and distribute, and the Lai Yupi Railway is the important line connecting the two provinces of Zhejiang and Jiangxi. This year, the government separately borrowed money from the banking group by mortgaging it to fill the construction and equipment needs. The total amount of the Yuping loan was 16 million yuan, the total amount of the Tongxi loan was 4.5 million yuan, and the total amount of the Han Yue loan was 1.5 million pounds in British gold. The Bank has shared a part of it with its peers. Now the construction of each road is progressing, and the Tongxi section of the Longhai Road has been completed. (2) Guarantee of Material Payments. Each road orders the materials needed for the improvement of engineering and equipment from foreign countries in installments. Foreign factories always need a letter of guarantee for payment from a reputable Chinese bank. The Bank uses this method to pay in installments, which can alleviate the financial resources of the road party and provide support for other equipment. Therefore, this year, it also jointly issued guarantees with its peers. To help the facilities of the road administration. The above is the general situation of the Bank's road administration services this year. However, a few years ago, due to the situation, the roads mostly defaulted on their debts. According to the investment principle, the Bank could not but temporarily suspend assistance. Recently, the government and the roads have actively reorganized their debts and developed their businesses, and can respect credit agreements and fulfill the terms and conditions. Therefore, they continue to invest to help construction. Also, this year, the Bank has also made considerable investments in the highways of various provinces, and it is shared with its peers.

(7) Personnel and Training of the Bank in Year 23

The work of modern banking business focuses on both quantity and quality. Considering the increase in the total amount, the staff will inevitably be used more, and in order to improve the quality, the staff must be trained. Now, the Bank's staff number comparison and staff training situation this year are briefly described below: (A) Staff Number Comparison. In Year 13, the total number of staff in the Bank was 553, an increase of 86 from the previous year. However, the Bank's employment policy is now mainly based on examinations. Except for certain necessary personnel in business, talents with considerable knowledge and experience are still used, and the rest are based on examinations to emphasize selection. Therefore, the newly added personnel this year accounted for 70% of the examinations. (B) Student Training. (1) Practical Training. Last year, the Bank recruited 11 graduates from the Department of Economics and Commerce of various universities in Pinghu and Shanghai. The Department of Economics of Nankai University specially set up a class for training on practical applications. This year's examination results were excellent and they were assigned to various banks to work. Also, this year, the authorities of various universities recommended a total of 15 excellent graduates from the Department of Economics and Commerce of the school. It is also advisable to add a little training on practical affairs. They are still hired by Nanda professors to provide corresponding guidance. After the examination, the results are excellent and they are assigned to various banks for trial use. (2) Field Practice. The Bank's Pinghu and Han branches have been busy with business and there are not enough people assigned to the above-mentioned personnel. Therefore, 36 graduates from high school and vocational schools were recruited from the three places and practiced directly in the banks. (3) Morning Village Service Training. In order to assist the rural economy, the Bank should train corresponding talents. This year, it happened to be the opening of the agricultural training class of the North China Agricultural Production Research and Improvement Society in Ding County. The Bank also sent people to the class to receive training together, and is now using it for agricultural services. (To be continued)

Weather Report 183

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong and the surrounding areas were cloudy with rain and a northeasterly wind, gradually clearing. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River were cloudy, with fog or drizzle in the morning. The wind came from the northeast to northwest and gradually cleared and turned sunny. There were cyclones and rain in the East China Sea, caused by a low pressure passing eastward or northeast eastward. The hurricane disappeared south of Dongsha Island. Its center was about within 120 miles of 18 degrees north latitude and 118 degrees east longitude at 2 pm yesterday. The wind force has not subsided. Also, within 24 hours before 3 pm yesterday, the temperature in this city was 63.9 at the highest and 54.1 at the lowest. On the same day last year, it was 74.5 at the highest and 57.9 at the lowest.

Sports News

The Old Ministry of Education's Physical Education Committee Held its Third Plenary Meeting Yesterday 185

More than twenty Physical Education Committee members and physical education directors from various provinces and cities attended. The directors reported in the morning, and the agenda items were discussed in the afternoon. Remaining items will be discussed at 9 a.m. today.

The Physical Education Committee of the Ministry of Education held its third plenary meeting at Jiaotong University, starting at 9 a.m. yesterday. Over twenty people attended, including physical education committee members and directors of physical education venues from various provinces and cities. The directors from various provinces and cities gave reports in the morning, and discussions began in the afternoon. Remaining items are scheduled to be discussed at Jiaotong University at 9 a.m. today. Details of the meeting are as follows:

Attendees

Attendees included Zhang Jiong, Director of the Social Education Department of the Ministry of Education; Section Chief Xu Yiqiao; Physical Education Committee members Zhang Boling, Hao Gengsheng, Shen Siliang, Zhang Zhijiang, Xu Minhui, Feng Dengke, Guan Songsheng (represented by Shen), Ma John, Xu Zhiyi, Wu Yunrui, Wu Zheng, Zhang Xinfu, Ma Liang, Yuan Dunli, Zhang Huilan, and others; physical education venue directors from various provinces and cities, including Zhang Zhongfan from Nanjing, Wang Zhuangfei (represented by Xiang Xianggao) from Shanghai, Gu Yuqi from Henan, Zhang Yixian from Qingdao, Yu Yongzuo from Jiangxi, Wu Bangwei from Jiangsu, Zhu Jiasheng from Zhejiang, Ke Nanshan from Hubei, Huang Fengqi from Hunan, Shang Shumei from Shandong, Zhao Wenzao from Hebei, and a total of over twenty people. Hao Gengsheng served as chairman, and Shao Rugan as recorder.

Director Zhang's Speech

The meeting began at 9 a.m. at the Jiaotong University gymnasium. After the customary formalities, the chairman gave a report, followed by Director Zhang Jiong of the Ministry of Education, who delivered a speech on behalf of Minister Wang, stating in brief: Minister Wang has already returned to Beijing to attend a political meeting and was therefore unable to attend in person. The National Physical Education Committee has been established for several years, and today's meeting is the third plenary session. Due to various difficulties in the past: (1) the committee members were scattered in different places, and many had other duties; (2) due to financial constraints, the meeting was delayed until today, and it really could not be postponed any longer. Many resolutions of the Standing Committee need to be discussed. Furthermore, the Ministry of Education feels that there are many difficulties in promoting national physical education, so we have gathered everyone to discuss solutions in order to increase the effectiveness of promotion. At the same time, we have invited the directors of physical education venues from various provinces and cities to participate in the meeting and share their opinions. Today, all countries in the world pay close attention to physical education, and our country is in a critical situation, so we should pay even more attention to it in order to save the country through physical education.

Reported Matters

Next were the reported matters: (1) Report of the Standing Committee: (A) Regarding the directive to all provinces and cities to select a normal school to establish a physical education department; (B) Regarding the measures for designating experimental areas for national martial arts curriculum standards; (C) Regarding the draft of the provisional regulations for physical education venues; (D) Regarding the report from the Shanxi Provincial Department of Education on the public physical education testing in Qingyuan and seven other counties; (E) Regarding the standards for national martial arts teaching materials for schools at all levels; (F) Regarding the inclusion of national martial arts in the entrance examination curriculum for schools at all levels; (2) Report by Committee Member Wu Yunrui: (A) Regarding the amendment of the regulations for athletic representatives in schools at all levels nationwide; (B) Testing the process of competitive sports; (3) Report by Committee Member Wu Zheng on the proposal to widely establish smaller-scale physical education venues; (4) Reports from the directors of physical education venues in various provinces and cities (attached below).

Discussion of Proposals

After the reports, lunch was taken at Jiaotong University's public dining hall. The meeting resumed at 2:30 p.m., chaired by Hao Gengsheng, to discuss the proposals: (1) Regarding the regulations for athletic representatives in schools at all levels nationwide, it was resolved to approve the amendment and submit it to the Ministry for approval and implementation after Committee Member Wu, the original proposer, has revised it; (2) Regarding the proposal to utilize the power of the military and police to assist public physical education to popularize physical education among all people, it was resolved to approve it in principle, and Xu Yiqiao and Zhang Dongping were appointed to work with Cheng Dengke, the original proposer, to revise and supplement it; (3) Regarding the request for public physical education institutions in various provinces and cities to assist in testing and revising the provisional standards for athletic performance, it was resolved to approve it and request the Ministry of Education to issue a directive to the departments and bureaus in various provinces and cities for implementation; (4) Regarding the directive to education departments and bureaus in various provinces and cities to hold athletic competitions and evaluations, it was resolved to approve it and request the Ministry of Education to issue a directive to the departments and bureaus in various provinces and cities for implementation; (5) Regarding the proposal to organize a health examination and physical education testing committee to examine the physical education and health of senior and junior high school students during this summer's entrance examinations in Jiangsu Province, in order to observe whether the current entrance examination system hinders the physical development of young people, it was resolved to retain it; (6) Regarding the opening of school physical education fields for public use, it was resolved to approve it in principle and hand it over to the Standing Committee for discussion; (7) Regarding the selection of physical education administrative personnel from various provinces, counties, and cities to accompany the World Games athletes to go abroad for observation, it was resolved to approve it in principle and the committee will recommend it to the Ministry of Education; (8) Regarding the request to standardize physical education terminology in our country, it was resolved to request the Ministry of Education to standardize and review it; (9) Shen Siliang made a temporary motion requesting the Ministry of Education to allow the National Sports Association to hold a physical education training course during the summer vacation this year, and for the Ministry to order departments and bureaus in various provinces and cities to send physical education teachers to attend, which was resolved to approve.

Athletic Standards

In the spring of the 23rd year [of the Republic, i.e., 1934], the Physical Education Committee resolved to appoint Wu Yunrui as a researcher to determine the standards for competitive sports. Testing was conducted in the summer and autumn of the same year among male students in junior and senior high schools in Beijing, totaling over 1,100 junior high school students and over 900 senior high school students. In the winter of the same year, Xu and Wu Xihong were entrusted to compile the following results: A. Junior High School Standards: (1) 50-meter dash: Excellent: 7.7 seconds or faster; Good: 8.2 seconds or faster; Average: 8.9 seconds or faster; Poor: Slower than 8.9 seconds; (2) 8-pound shot put: Excellent: 7.34 meters or farther; Good: 6.32 meters or farther; Average: 5.25 meters or farther; Poor: Shorter than 5.25 meters; (3) Standing long jump: Excellent: 1.97 meters or farther; Good: 1.805 meters or farther; Average: 1.61 meters or farther; Poor: Shorter than 1.61 meters; (4) High jump: Excellent: 1.23 meters or higher; Good: 1.14 meters or higher; Average: 1.01 meters or higher; Poor: Lower than 1.01 meters; B. Senior High School Standards: (1) 100-meter dash: Excellent: 13.8 seconds or faster; Good: 15.1 seconds or faster; Average: 16.1 seconds or faster; Poor: Slower than 16.1 seconds; (2) Standing long jump: Excellent: 2.14 meters or farther; Good: 1.99 meters or farther; Average: 1.81 meters or farther; Poor: Shorter than 1.81 meters; (3) Shot put (8 pounds): Excellent: 7.72 meters or farther; Good: 6.45 meters or farther; Average: 5.69 meters or farther; Poor: Shorter than 5.69 meters; (4) High jump: Excellent: 1.2 meters or higher; Good: 1.14 meters or higher; Average: 1.06 meters or higher; Poor: Lower than 1.06 meters.

Two Public Banquets

At noon yesterday, Jiaotong University hosted a banquet for all committee members at the university, where Qiu Weiyu, Dean of Academic Affairs of the university, and Zhong Weicheng, Chairman of the Physical Education Committee, delivered welcoming speeches, followed by speeches by Hao Gengsheng and Director Zhang. The banquet ended around 2 p.m. At 5:30 p.m., the Ministry of Education hosted a banquet for all committee members on the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA, where Director Zhang and Inspector Hao delivered speeches. The banquet ended around 9 p.m.

Meeting Continues Today

The meeting will continue today at 9 a.m. at the Jiaotong University gymnasium to discuss: (1) Provisional Regulations for Physical Education Venues; (2) Request for Stipulating the National Physical Education Work Outline; (3) Request for Including Physical Education in the Entrance Examination Curriculum of Sun Yat-sen Schools; (4) Request for Stipulating the Certification Measures for Physical Education Teachers in Primary and Secondary Schools; (5) Temporary Motions; (6) Adjournment.

Reports from the Directors 186

Nanjing: Zhang Zhongfan, Director of the Nanjing Public Physical Education Venue, reported that although the Nanjing Physical Education Venue is located in the urban area of Nanjing, it is under the jurisdiction of Jiangsu Province. The venue covers 80.5 mu (approximately 13.3 acres), which is located in the southeast of the city, which is not very convenient. The annual funding is 14,000 yuan. The organization is divided into two departments: guidance and administration. In 1928, the number of people entering the venue for sports was 40 to 70 per day, which increased to 140 to 180 in 1930. The equipment of the physical education venue is not very complete, and the army often borrows the venue for exercises. Now it has been restricted to supply in the morning, and the maximum limit is until 3 pm. The career is gradually progressing, but it is hoped that the venue will be jointly operated by the Provincial Education Department, the Nanjing Municipal Government, and the Ministry of Education, so that it can become a trial physical education venue suitable for the city.

Henan: Gu Yuqi, Director of the Kaifeng Physical Education Venue in Henan Province, reported that the venue began construction during the 16th North China Games in Henan in 1931 and was completed in 1932. The construction cost was over 100,000 yuan. The form is relatively old and there are many inconveniences. The surrounding area is more than 120 mu (approximately 19.8 acres), divided into track and field and ball games. The stands and the rostrum are built in the middle of the ball field, with five tennis courts, three basketball courts, two volleyball courts, one football field, and a children's playground in the track and field field. There is also room for building a swimming pool and a gymnasium, which is being planned by the Provincial Education Department. The funding was more than 500 yuan per month in 1932, which increased to 713 yuan in 1933. The organization is divided into two departments: guidance and administration. In terms of career, the annual folk sports meeting is the most grand.

Qingdao: Zhang Yixian, Director of the Qingdao Public Physical Education Venue, reported that the venue was built during the North China Games in 1932, with a cost of 160,000 yuan. The area is more than 120 hectares, with a circumference of 400 meters. The stands can accommodate 20,000 people. The track and field field and ball field are complete. The funding is relatively fixed. Qingdao's education fee is 600,000 yuan per year, of which 60,000 yuan is for social education. The social education fee allocates 12,000 yuan for physical education. The physical education venue's funding is 5,000 yuan per year. In terms of career, all kinds of attention is paid to the fact that Qingdao's physical education is quite developed.

Shanghai: Xiang Xianggao reported on behalf of the Shanghai First Physical Education Venue. The venue was opened in 1913 and originally belonged to the county. It was transferred to the city in 1928 and managed by the Education Bureau. The current annual funding is 9,552 yuan. The venue covers 26 mu (approximately 4.3 acres), with an actual area of 20 mu (approximately 3.3 acres) excluding the buildings. The four sides are all city houses and cannot be expanded. The internal equipment is simple, with one football field, one basketball court, two tennis courts, and one martial arts room. The organization is the same as other venues. All aspects of the career are paid attention to, but it is a pity that the venue is small and there are many athletes.

Jiangsu: Wu Bangwei, Director of the Zhenjiang Physical Education Venue in Jiangsu Province, reported that the venue's annual funding is 17,000 yuan. Although it is more than other places, it still feels lacking in terms of career. The organization is divided into two departments: guidance and promotion. A lot of promotion has been done in terms of career, but how to make people in the industrial and commercial sectors have the opportunity to participate is hoped to be paid attention to together, and the physical education career is only solely responsible by the physical education venue, which is weak.

Zhejiang: Zhu Jiasheng, Director of the Hangzhou Physical Education Venue in Zhejiang Province, reported that the venue was built during the National Games in 1930 and has now been expanded. It is quite suitable for large-scale sports meets. The funding is more than 900 yuan per month, and it has now become a place where various sports meets are borrowed. There are 16 physical education venues in various counties in Zhejiang Province that belong to the counties, and 160 that belong to the folk education centers in various counties. Although the number is large, many are nominal.

Hubei: Ke Nanshan, Director of the Wuchang Physical Education Venue in Hubei Province, reported that the venue already existed during the National Games in 1924, but it was not managed until 1931 and became a horse racing venue for soldiers. It was not until 1933 that Chen Qibao, Director of the Education Department, paid attention to physical education and established the venue. The monthly funding is 300 yuan, which increased to 360 yuan in 1934. The equipment includes three basketball courts, two volleyball courts, four tennis courts, and one football field and track and field field each. There is a great lack of a gymnasium and swimming pool.

Hunan: Huang Fengqi, Director of the Changsha Physical Education Venue in Hunan Province, reported that the venue's annual funding is 1,700 yuan, which is also subject to an 80% discount. It was established in 1930. The venue is very large. Every time a career is held, it cooperates with other sports organizations. It has greatly promoted public sports in the banking, book, and seafarer sectors. It is now preparing to host the Central China Games next year, so it plans to expand its equipment.

Shandong: Shang Shumei, Director of the Jinan Physical Education Venue in Shandong Province, reported that the venue already existed in 1923, and the scale was larger in 1931. The construction cost was 80,000 yuan, covering an area of more than 100 mu (approximately 16.5 acres). The funding is 12,180 yuan, which has now been reduced to 10,824 yuan, with more than 900 yuan per month. The public who come to the venue include students, civil servants, and other sectors.

Hebei: Zhao Wenzao, Director of the Tianjin Physical Education Venue in Hebei Province, reported that the venue was built for the North China Games. The scale is relatively large and is not far from Tianjin City. The environment is very good. Except for the swimming pool, the equipment is complete. It is now kept by the Hebei Provincial Education Department, so the Education Department sent a custodian. The funding is 388 yuan, or 4,560 yuan per year. The area is 200 mu (approximately 33 acres). The construction cost, including the foundation, is 320,000 yuan. The venue is large, and there are many buildings, but there are few staff members, so it is difficult to manage. It is now being used as an auditorium for provincial and municipal conferences and as a school sports venue.

Jiangxi: Yu Yongzuo, Director of the Nanchang Physical Education Venue in Jiangxi Province, reported that the venue was reorganized and established in 1933, with 10,068 yuan per year. A lot of work has been done in the past two years. The Education Department can also have an additional subsidy of 10,000 yuan per year. The equipment includes four football fields, seven basketball courts, six tennis courts, one martial arts field, one handball field, one children's playground, one small swimming pool, and one equipment field for adults. The stands can accommodate 3,000 people. It is now planned to build a gymnasium and swimming pool, with a budget of 50,000 yuan. More than 1,500 people come to the venue every day.

Guangdong: Xu Minhui reported on behalf of the Guangdong Provincial Sports Venue. The venue is managed by the Education Department's Physical Education Committee and has no director. It covers an area of 200 mu (approximately 33 acres). The sports field has been drawn, and the seats can accommodate 3,000 people. The remaining equipment is being planned, with a prepared cost of more than 3 million yuan. The current monthly funding is 1,500 yuan, which is allocated by the provincial government. Public sports have a considerable development in Guangdong, and military sports are particularly developed.

Wu Bangwei Talks About Improving Social Sports 187

Start with expanding and reorganizing existing sports venues. Existing social education institutions should be arranged with sports environments.

Wu Bangwei, Director of the Zhenjiang Physical Education Venue in Jiangsu Province, came to Shanghai this time to attend the joint meeting of sports directors from various provinces convened by the Ministry of Education. A Shanghai social reporter specially visited him yesterday. According to him, his views on improving social sports are very detailed, and are recorded as follows:

Fundamental Problems

Mr. Wu first said that the fundamental problems of improving social sports: (1) The entire social sports cannot be borne by a few sports people. How can the responsible persons of local administrative education be able to promote it with great effort? (2) In addition to the sports venues, there is no designated amount to seek development in social sports funds. Comparing the population of a city with the funds of a sports venue, the average cost per person per year is only a few cents or a few cents, and of course it cannot be developed. How to ensure that local social sports funds have a fixed budget? (3) The social living environment is like this, and the public's understanding of sports is like that. Social sports facilities do not have a correct object. How to enable the industrial and commercial sectors to have a fixed time every day to engage in sports?

Improvement Methods

Mr. Wu then talked about the improvement methods, saying that before the above-mentioned fundamental problems are solved, large-scale expansion of sports will definitely fail, be ineffective, and uneconomical. Therefore, expanding and reorganizing the existing sports venues, and setting up sports venues and equipment in existing social education institutions and public venues, is a suitable method for improving social sports today. Expanding and reorganizing existing sports venues must enrich economic equipment, use excellent talents, determine the minimum work items and the number of careers, and pay attention to children's sports with appropriate literacy and labor training. At the same time, students in public schools and private schools who lack sports training should be allowed to go to the sports venues at regular intervals to find a fixed object.

Social Education Institutions

As for setting up sports venues in existing social education institutions and public venues, first, all social education institutions such as folk and agricultural education halls should set up small-scale sports venues, which are managed by the recreation department. Second, increase the funds allocated to the Wu Agricultural Education Hall and designate them for sports and health facilities. Third, refer to the financial equipment situation and formulate career standards. Fourth, the public who receive fixed training at the folk and agricultural education halls should be given the opportunity to play games and sports appropriately, with a duration of seven or five minutes to twenty minutes each day or each time. Fifth, parks and special sports departments should set up ball fields and children's play equipment.

School Aspects

Mr. Wu finally said that in terms of the current school sports venues, it is not enough to provide extracurricular activities for the students of the school. It is actually difficult to open them to the public. All management guidance and consumption are extra things. Moreover, issuing an order to open the school without anyone to preside over and promote it, the public may not go to sports. However, it may be a preliminary attempt, that is, any sports competition held by the school should set up an open group. All registration procedures should be entrusted to the sports venues for handling. The school venues are used to occupy a part of the time, so that the public can have more opportunities to participate. Only in this way can it be successful and can we further plan to open school sports venues.

Jiangwan Six-Mile Cross-Country Run 188

Fourteen teams of Chinese and foreigners participated. Waters was unable to come to Shanghai to participate due to an event. The list of participants from each team was released yesterday.

The Jiangwan six-mile team cross-country championship organized by the Westerners' Sports Association is scheduled to be held at 10:30 a.m. on the 14th (Sunday) at the west gate of Hongkou Park. There were originally as many as fifteen teams participating in the competition, but Waters, the champion of the previous edition, originally intended to come to Shanghai to participate, but unfortunately, he was unable to do so due to an event and had to give up. Therefore, only fourteen teams actually competed. There are five Chinese teams, including Shanghai United Team A and B, the Chinese Sports Association, the Huaguang Track and Field Team, and the Hongkou Cross-Country Team. The Westerners include Ennis Teams A, B, C, and D, French Army Teams A and B, Westerners' Sports Association Teams A and B, and the Russian Emigrants Team. It is generally agreed that the Russian Emigrants Team, Ennis, the French Army, and Shanghai United Team A are the strongest this time. However, Shanghai United Team has famous Jiangnan players such as Wang Zhilin, He Baoshan, Zhang Liang, Jin Zhongkang, etc., but they have no experience in the mud roads, fields, and ditches that the cross-country run passes through. Moreover, the Chinese have always been naturally inferior and lazy to practice. It is not easy to compete with experienced and strong enemies for a day. Therefore, our country has very little hope for the championship in this competition. The list of each team is recorded as follows:

National Southeast University, Great China University Alumni Association Representative Meeting Resolves to Request Alma Mater Authorities to Promote Inherent Spirit, Elects Wang Shufang, Xue Zhongtai, etc. as Directors and Supervisors 196

The first members' representative meeting convened by the National Southeast University, Great China University Alumni Association was held at the association's auditorium on the 4th and 5th of this month, with one opening ceremony, one preparatory meeting, and two formal meetings. More than seventy representatives from branches at home and abroad attended. Zhang Tingxiu chaired the meeting, with Wang Shufang, Jiang Jianbai, Yu Xilai, and Chen Shizhen as co-chairs, and Liu Zonglie and Sun Guangyu as recorders. The resolutions and election results of the meeting are recorded below: (1) A letter requesting the alma mater authorities to maintain the inherent spirit of sincerity, simplicity, diligence, and prudence and continue to promote it, without overemphasizing material construction, was passed. (2) Considering that material construction has already been established, the school environment is still suitable, and it is not appropriate to build a new school during this time of national crisis and spend public funds, a proposal to request the government to stop the school relocation plan was passed. (3) A letter requesting the alma mater to eliminate redundant staff and employ as many alumni as possible to serve as faculty members was passed. (4) A letter requesting the General Association to review the suggestions made by the previous general meetings and executive committees to the alma mater that have not been adopted and to promptly promote their implementation was passed. (5) A letter requesting the alma mater to immediately implement economic transparency and submit a copy of each annual budget and final account to the association for the purpose of contributing to the development of the alma mater was passed. (6) A resolution that local branches should be named "National Southeast University, Great China University Alumni Association, [Location] Branch" to show uniformity was passed. (9) How to raise funds to provide educational relief to the children of deceased alumni was resolved to be referred to the next board of directors to develop a detailed plan. (10) How to jointly organize a career placement agency with the school to seek employment opportunities for alumni was resolved to be referred to the next board of directors to develop a method promptly. (11) Collecting donations from branches and individuals was resolved to be handled by the next board of directors. (12) Holding fundraising events to enrich the association's headquarters facilities and add books was resolved to be handled by the next board of directors. Students Use Domestic Products, Scheduled to Hold a Swearing-in Ceremony, Simultaneously Exhibiting Students' Domestic Products, and Soliciting Articles for General Mobilization and Persuasion 200

According to the Central News Agency, the "Student Domestic Product Year Promotion Federation," organized by industrial, commercial, and educational circles in the city, has decided to hold a student domestic product use swearing-in ceremony at the Municipal Government Auditorium on the 18th of this month. At the same time, a student domestic product exhibition will be held. On that day, all students in the city will be generally mobilized to form a persuasion team and launch a student essay contest to expand publicity. The Central News Agency reporter inquired about the details as follows:

Reporting Process Scheduled to be Held

The Student Domestic Product Year Promotion Federation yesterday submitted a report to the Municipal Education Bureau, stating that it was requesting instructions to be issued to various schools to select representatives to participate in the swearing-in. The association noted that the dumping of foreign goods was increasing daily, and the amount of import surplus was alarming. If this continued, domestic industry and commerce would inevitably go bankrupt, and the future was worrying. Therefore, the association jointly organized this association with public groups in the city, hoping that students' inherent patriotism could lead all circles in promoting domestic products to save the interests of the country. The progress of the association has been reported on file. It has now been decided to hold a swearing-in ceremony for representatives of all large, medium, and small schools in the city at the Municipal Government Auditorium at 2 p.m. on April 18th. The Mayor is invited to attend and preside over the oath to set a good example and facilitate the process. Therefore, the Bureau is requested to notify all schools to select at least five representatives per hundred people, led by faculty members, to attend the meeting on time. The attached lyrics and registration forms are also sent for distribution to various schools. Before the swearing-in ceremony, the lyrics should be rehearsed to be sung at the time. The registration forms should be filled in and reported to the association within a limited time. It is believed that the authorities of various schools have always been enthusiastic about promoting domestic products and will certainly support this grand event. The association will be grateful if the request is approved.

Exhibition of Supplies Enthusiastic Participation

The association also decided to hold a student supplies exhibition at the Municipal Government Auditorium on that day. The exhibition period is tentatively set for one day, and may be extended if necessary. The association has now begun to solicit products from domestic manufacturers in the city for display. All products participating in the exhibition must be accompanied by clear descriptions and trademarks, but the style is not specified. As for the samples, each manufacturer can design and decorate them freely to enhance the visual effect. Manufacturers who wish to print publicity materials and gifts at the exhibition must send samples to the association for contact in advance. It is reported that more than 40 well-known domestic manufacturers have been recruited, and several applications for registration are still being received every day. It is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Expand Publicity Solicit Manuscripts

In order to expand publicity, the association will not only specially contract various newspapers to publish temporary special editions, but also send letters to schools at all levels to solicit manuscripts. The topic of the essay is determined by the author. First, the principals of each school select good works and send them to the association with a letter. Each school is limited to two volumes. The essay must be based on the student's personal standpoint, expressing opinions and contributing practical methods. The style of writing is not limited, but it must be written in regular script with new-style punctuation. If foreign paper is used, it will be rejected. The deadline for submissions is from now until April 15th. Manuscripts should be sent to the association at No. 80, Longhua Road. Prizes are available to encourage participation.

Organize Persuasion Teams Start Soliciting

In order to awaken citizens to use domestic products and promote domestic products, the association will not only hold a swearing-in ceremony and exhibit domestic products on that day, but also mobilize all students and boy scouts in the city to organize student persuasion teams and persuade people along the way to expand publicity. The association has sent letters to the Municipal Education Bureau and the Shanghai Boy Scouts Association to instruct schools to handle this matter. The association's target for recruiting members since the start has been 500,000 people, and it is reported that the number has exceeded half.
